CC   -!- FUNCTION: Gametocyte surface protein required for male/female
CC       gamete fusion. Also required for male gamete exflagellation and
CC       interaction with erythrocytes. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:16879650}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Heterodimer; heterodimerizes with PF45/48.
CC   -!- SUBCELLULAR LOCATION: Cell surface. Cell membrane.
CC   -!- DEVELOPMENTAL STAGE: Specifically expressed in gametocytes.
CC   -!- MISCELLANEOUS: Promising transmission-blocking vaccine candidate:
CC       targeting the protein would prevent transmission of the parasite
CC       decreasing the malaria burden.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Contains 14 6-Cys domains. {ECO:0000305}.

CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Heterodimer; heterodimerizes with PF41. May form an
CC       antiparallel heterodimer with PF41.
CC   -!- SUBCELLULAR LOCATION: Merozoite surface protein P12: Cell surface.
CC       Cell membrane {ECO:0000305}; Lipid-anchor, GPI-anchor
CC       {ECO:0000305}. Note=Present on the surface of merozoite.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:22848665}.
CC   -!- SUBCELLULAR LOCATION: Merozoite surface protein P12, processed
CC       form: Cell surface. Cell membrane. Note=Shed from the merozoite
CC       surface. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:22848665}.
CC   -!- DEVELOPMENTAL STAGE: Specifically present in asexual blood stage
CC       parasites. First detected in the trophozoite stage, 30-40 hours
CC       post-invasion (HPI) and the proteins reaches peak expression in
CC       schizont stage, 40-48 HPI. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:16203726,
CC       ECO:0000269|PubMed:22848665}.
CC   -!- PTM: Processed into a soluble form. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:22848665}.
CC   -!- DISRUPTION PHENOTYPE: No visible phenotype. Parasites grow at
CC       normal rates in vitro. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:22848665}.
CC   -!- MISCELLANEOUS: Does not have erythrocyte-receptor-binding ability.
CC       {ECO:0000305|PubMed:22848665}.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Contains 2 6-Cys domains. {ECO:0000305}.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Catalyzes the radical-mediated insertion of two sulfur
CC       atoms into the C-6 and C-8 positions of the octanoyl moiety bound
CC       to the lipoyl domains of lipoate-dependent enzymes, thereby
CC       converting the octanoylated domains into lipoylated derivatives.
CC       {ECO:0000255|HAMAP-Rule:MF_03123, ECO:0000269|PubMed:15225307}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: Protein N(6)-(octanoyl)lysine + 2 sulfur-
CC       (sulfur carrier) + 2 S-adenosyl-L-methionine + 2 reduced [2Fe-2S]
CC       ferredoxin = protein N(6)-(lipoyl)lysine + 2 (sulfur carrier) + 2
CC       L-methionine + 2 5'-deoxyadenosine + 2 oxidized [2Fe-2S]
CC       ferredoxin. {ECO:0000255|HAMAP-Rule:MF_03123}.
CC   -!- COFACTOR:
CC       Name=[4Fe-4S] cluster; Xref=ChEBI:CHEBI:49883;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000255|HAMAP-Rule:MF_03123};
CC       Note=Binds 2 [4Fe-4S] clusters per subunit. One cluster is
CC       coordinated with 3 cysteines and an exchangeable S-adenosyl-L-
CC       methionine. {ECO:0000255|HAMAP-Rule:MF_03123};
CC   -!- PATHWAY: Protein modification; protein lipoylation via endogenous
CC       pathway; protein N(6)-(lipoyl)lysine from octanoyl-[acyl-carrier-

RL   Science 340:984-987(2013).
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Mediates evasion of the mosquito innate immune response
CC       by suppressing midgut nitration responses that are critical to
CC       activate the mosquito complement system. It is unclear whether the
CC       protein has a role in passive evasion by making the parasite
CC       invisible to the mosquito immune system, acts as a decoy to
CC       prevent recognition of another surface protein or anchors the
CC       decoy protein. Not required for female fertility.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:16824624, ECO:0000269|PubMed:23661646}.
CC   -!- SUBCELLULAR LOCATION: Cell surface {ECO:0000269|PubMed:16824624}.
CC       Cell membrane {ECO:0000305|PubMed:16824624}; Lipid-anchor, GPI-
CC       anchor {ECO:0000305|PubMed:16824624}. Note=Specifically present on
CC       the surface of female gametocytes. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:16824624}.
CC   -!- DEVELOPMENTAL STAGE: Expressed only in female gametocytes
CC       following emergence from red blood cells.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:16824624}.
CC   -!- DISRUPTION PHENOTYPE: Reduced parasite survival in the mosquito.
CC       Parasites produce normal numbers of oocysts when included in the
CC       blood meal of the mosquito vector. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:16824624,
CC       ECO:0000269|PubMed:23661646}.
CC   -!- MISCELLANEOUS: Exhibits a high rate of non-synonymous polymorphism
CC       is different strains, suggesting that it adapts to different
CC       Anopheles vector species. {ECO:0000305|PubMed:23661646}.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Contains 2 6-Cys domains. {ECO:0000305}.
